The successful Star side was Latter, Blades (sub Fovargue), Slack, Murphy, Wilson, Slight, Tokely, Williamson, Evans, Thomson (sub Ippolito), Clipston.\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<noscript>\n\t\t\t\t\t&lt;img src=\"http://res.cloudinary.com/jpress/image/fetch/w_444,f_auto,ar_3:2,c_fill/http://www.peterboroughtoday.co.uk/webimage/1.7924476.1492695980!/image/image.jpg\" class=\"teaser-lead__image\" alt=\"Pictured 40 years ago is the Western Star team after winning the Hunts Colts League\u0019s David Wright Shield competition.
